[*] === Optional APUSYS run_cmd VPU IOVA chained probe ===
[*] Mode: mem_create imports HardwareBuffer to get IOVA, writes a libneuron-style XRP settings buffer into that IOVA, then the VPU request references settings/output/data sections.
[*] XRP settings shape: plane_valid_tail output_size=0x40 data_desc_size=0xc include_data_desc=true.
[*] Split target: XRP data descriptor and native VPU plane0 MVA point at different IOVA offsets.
[*] Nonzero XRP code section: opcode=10003 name=XTENSA_ANN_VERSION op_size=0x1c8 inputs=0 outputs=1 operands=[0]
[*] Native VPU descriptor mode: buffer_count=5, all five buffers point to the wrapper DSP command/settings buffer.
[*] VPU descriptor metadata mode: libvpu_metadata_settings5
[*] XRP command flags override: settings[0]=0x5 (wrapper send state uses 0x5).
[*] VPU request settings length override: request+0x38=0x68 (wrapper DSP command buffer size is 0x68).
[*] VPU settings property disabled: request+0x38/request+0x40 are zeroed, matching the target wrapper path where CreateVpuRequest only adds buffers.
[*] Code/input first word override: code+0x00=0x2713
[*] Native descriptor payload size override: size=0x80
